<date>1612158159014< /date><rating>3<//rating>< Review>
The food isn‚Äôt bad, and will satisfy your craving for banh mi and a variety of snacks at cheap prices . But the poor service, poor covid safety, and long wait is enough to stop me from coming back (at least to this location). Would recommend the cleaner THH restaurant chain instead.

Food:
Grilled pork Banh mi was tasty with generous portion of meat. The egg rolls were nicely fried, and peppery. Also got some chicken pate chaud at really cheap prices. Good but a bit salty, and could use more meat. They sell their baguettes too which is nice to bring home to snack on.

Downsides:
- Covid measures are not being enforced well here. The sign says no more than 10 customers inside and there were definitely at least 30 customers crammed inside when I got there.
-Workers are eating inside maskless on lunch breaks. Also the workers are inside yelling a lot so that can‚Äôt be great even with masks.
- service is below average. While I was trying to order the cashier was having an entire side conversation with another customer and interrupted me 4x to the point I was laughing in disbelief. Then got impatient with us  as we ordered with the language barrier.
- wait times are really long when there‚Äôs a line. We waited in line for 10min, then another 20min for food. Not the ‚Äúquick‚Äù snack we thought it would be.<//Review>

Their prices are not any better than other places. Their food are not the best either. A convenient place to pickup different kinds of Vietnamese food at once.< /review>

<Text>I am totally addicted to this place. They have fresh baked items everyday. The earlier you go the better and fresher. It seems no matter what time I go, there is a line, but it is well worth the wait. The offer baguettes, pho, chicken wings, bahn mi sandwiches (I highly recommend with the veggies INSIDE for the full experience of this glorious sandwich. They also have some desserts I haven't tried yet and I'm still exploring all they have to offer.

When you go, you have to get the BOBA milk, green, or thai tea. The also offer more than just boba to add to your drinks.  Just get in there and try it.  Oh and did I mention the teas are BOGO FREE? $3.00 for the regular size, $3.50 for the large. Do yourself a favor and spend the extra $.50 for the large because with the size of the straws to suck up the BOBAs, the tea will be gone quickly.

Happy eating!<//Text>< Gmap_id>

<Response>None</Response><UserId.>105949222955452550306</UserId.><Review>Best burgers I have ever had.

The atmosphere is great, its not what you would expect for how good it is though. They have TVs displaying sports or news or whatever else, which doesn't really bother me one way or the other. The owners are the nicest people. They love to come and talk to you like you were a close friend, which is amazing. They are down to earth, and love to hear your honest feedback. They are always thinking up new ideas to make the customers happier.

Their location is a bit strange, and its easy to miss where you pull in. I am a new driver though, and I could do it easily. The location has a very homey feel to it, which I adore.

So! The food. Their menu, which I heard that they are freshening up a bit, looks a little daunting. It isn't. It is in big font, which makes it easy to read, but makes it look kinda like the menu is bigger than it is. What I got this last time was the make your own burger. You get to choose your meat, cheese, toppings, insides of the burger, your side, the works. I got my burger medium rare, and it was delicious. I have leftovers waiting for me in the fridge it filled me up so well! (They've even won awards as far as I know!)

These wonderful people need to see some more love. They are incredible, and so very sweet. We need to get the news out there about them.

I hope my review helped with the decision to eat there!<//Review></record></dataset><record>

<Rate>4<//Rate><review>Boomerang's is a unique burger joint in the Clairemont Mesa area. It's not very noticeable from the main road, and even from the parking lot, the entrance is hidden away in a little courtyard. First, the criticisms: The building seems older and not well taken care of. This is emphasized by the hodgepodge decorations (but not in a good way). There was also no music (though I did notice ceiling speakers), which contributed to making the ambiance awkwardly quiet since there were few guests when we went and the restaurant is surprisingly large. On the positive side, our waiter (Jose) was very friendly and attentive. I had a 1/2lb Bad Breath Burger with Chilli Pepper Onion Rings. I love garlic; so, having garlic mixed into the Patty was amazing. Staying true to it's name, the cheese of choice is gorgonzola, and it is slathers with just enough fresh horseradish. Grilled onions galore top the creation, and on the side comes a creamy garlic-horseradish mayo. The Chilli Pepper Onion Rings have a wonderful crunch and get an added kick by the jalapeno topping. It comes with habanero ketchup which is good, though not as spicy as I hoped for, given the name. Overall, it's a delicious meal in an okay space. But, I think it's worth a shot!</review><pics>None</pics><response>None<//response><gmap_id>0x80dc0058556d6483:0xc63269d1910bc67e< /gmap_id></record>

1483308972460< /time>
<gmapID>0x80dc0058556d6483:0xc63269d1910bc67e<//gmapID>< text>
We ordered 2 apps and 2 entrees with salads. Approx 68 bucks with 15% tip.
The salads were ok. The rest of the food was awful.
I called the restaurant to see if the chef had a stroke or something, and let them know the food was well below expectations.
The man who answered the phone interrupted me repeatedly and said I was being "mean" when I told him the mac and cheese was a soggy old inedible mess with separated cheese sauce- totally microwaved.
He declared that all was "made to order" and when I suggested he hire a new chef (I have to now assume I was speaking to the sensitive chef?) he tried to blame the yelp eat24 driver on the poor quality food.
I'll post pics of the Philly cheesesteak- lettuce and tomatoes- whyyy?? And a big ole hunk of overdone steak, apparently couldn't be bothered to slice it thin- or at all.
Burger- super soggy bun. When an order is going out for delivery you should know how to package it.
And the worst offender- which made me put down my fork and start this review- the mac and cheese. Disgusting. Mushy, greasy, separated sauce and pasta was cooked to death.
Calamari- frozen strips. I want rings and tentacles, you know- real food.
All of it was flavorless and overdone. Huge portions of low quality product. Oh boy!<//text>

< text>
This place is the best. It's hard to find authentic Mexican food in Simi Valley but here it is. The tri-tip is to die for! The burrito is good like a carne asada burrito but lately the sauce has been spicy so watch out! Also great homemade salsa. Good selection of Mexican bottled drinks as well as Fountain drinks. I love the spanish music, it's just like being at my Grandma's house. It doesn't get more authentic than this. I like the decor it's kind of Southwestern. Check it out you won't be disappointed.</text>
